START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD EQUALS START_AGG_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW SUM(OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD) AS OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS EQUALS START_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ( SELECT OUTER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE (((STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND (((NOT (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES)) AND ((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%')) AND NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL OR STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE) AND NOT (STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND BOOL_FIELD = false))) OR ((((STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD AND NOT (STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)))) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL AND STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD = true)) OR ((NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE) AND (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST )) AND BOOL_FIELD = true)))) LIMIT 1 ) END_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ) END_AGG_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;

START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD NOT_EQUALS START_AGG_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW MIN(OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD) AS OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE ((NOT (((NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%')) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)))) OR (((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL OR (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES))) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD IS NULL)))) OR (NOT ((STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES' AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) ) END_AGG_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;

START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_IN_FIELD IN START_IN_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW OUTER_SUBQUERY_IN_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE ((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL AND NOT (STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) AND BOOL_FIELD != true)) AND (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) ) END_IN_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;

START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD NOT_EQUALS START_AGG_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW MAX(OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD) AS OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS NOT_EQUALS START_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ( SELECT OUTER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = true OR (STRING_FIELD <> STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES))) LIMIT 1 ) END_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ) END_AGG_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE EXISTS START_EXISTS_SUBQUERY ( SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE EXISTS START_EXISTS_SUBQUERY ( SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE NOT (((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) ) END_EXISTS_SUBQUERY ) END_EXISTS_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD NOT_EQUALS START_AGG_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW AVG(OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD) AS OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS NOT_EQUALS START_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ( SELECT OUTER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD != true OR STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) LIMIT 1 ) END_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ) END_AGG_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD NOT_EQUALS START_AGG_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW MAX(OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD) AS OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD EQUALS START_AGG_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW MAX(OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD) AS OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE EXISTS START_EXISTS_SUBQUERY ( SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE ((((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES)) OR ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR NOT (STRING_FIELD IS NULL)))) AND (((STRING_FIELD IS NULL) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR ((STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES AND NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST )))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)))) OR (NOT ((((BOOL_FIELD = true AND NUMERIC_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) OR ((STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE)))))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != false OR ((STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES')) AND (STRING_FIELD IS NULL))) ) END_EXISTS_SUBQUERY ) END_AGG_SUBQUERY ) END_AGG_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_IN_FIELD NOT IN START_IN_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW OUTER_SUBQUERY_IN_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS EQUALS START_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ( SELECT OUTER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE (NOT ((NOT ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND ((NOT (NOT (((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))))) AND ((STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))))) OR (NOT (NOT (((BOOL_FIELD != true OR STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE STRING_VALUES))))) LIMIT 1 ) END_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ) END_IN_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE NOT EXISTS START_EXISTS_SUBQUERY ( SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD EQUALS START_AGG_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW SUM(OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD) AS OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE (BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD LIKE '%STRING_VALUES%') ) END_AGG_SUBQUERY ) END_EXISTS_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE EXISTS START_EXISTS_SUBQUERY ( SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS NOT_EQUALS START_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ( SELECT OUTER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND ((BOOL_FIELD OR STRING_FIELD IS NULL)) OR ((STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ) AND NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD NOT LIKE '%STRING_VALUES' AND NOT (BOOL_FIELD))) LIMIT 1 ) END_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ) END_EXISTS_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE NOT EXISTS START_EXISTS_SUBQUERY ( SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_IN_FIELD IN START_IN_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW OUTER_SUBQUERY_IN_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS EQUALS START_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ( SELECT OUTER_SUBQUERY_FIELDS FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE NOT (NOT ((((((STRING_FIELD >= STRING_VALUES) AND (STRING_FIELD LIKE STRING_VALUES) AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) AND ((NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE OR STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) OR (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false AND (STRING_FIELD > STRING_VALUES) AND (NOT ((STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES) OR (STRING_FIELD <= STRING_VALUES)))))) AND (NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL) AND (NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE))))) OR (((STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES AND NUMERIC_FIELD = NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE AND NOT (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)))))) LIMIT 1 ) END_FIELDS_COMPARISON_SUBQUERY ) END_IN_SUBQUERY ) END_EXISTS_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE NOT EXISTS START_EXISTS_SUBQUERY ( SELECT * FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE (STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != false OR STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) ) END_EXISTS_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD NOT_EQUALS START_AGG_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW SUM(OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD) AS OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE NOT ((NOT (NOT ((((BOOL_FIELD != true AND (NOT (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES)) AND (STRING_FIELD IS NOT NULL))) OR ((BOOL_FIELD != true OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) AND (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE))) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = false OR NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL)) OR ((NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL))) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD IS NOT NULL)) AND ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)))))) AND (((NOT ((NUMERIC_FIELD <= NUMERIC_VALUE AND STRING_FIELD != STRING_VALUES AND BOOL_FIELD != true))) OR (NOT ((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) OR STRING_FIELD IS NULL)))) OR ((((NOT (BOOL_FIELD)) AND ((STRING_FIELD LIKE 'STRING_VALUES%' AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE))) OR (((NOT (BOOL_FIELD) AND NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) AND ((BOOL_FIELD = true AND NUMERIC_FIELD BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)))) AND (((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD IN ( LIST ))) AND (NOT ((STRING_FIELD = STRING_VALUES AND (NUMERIC_FIELD > NUMERIC_VALUE) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD < NUMERIC_VALUE)))))))) ) END_AGG_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_IN_FIELD IN START_IN_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW OUTER_SUBQUERY_IN_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS OUTER_PRIMARY_KEY WHERE ((BOOL_FIELD != true AND STRING_FIELD IS NULL)) OR ((BOOL_FIELD = true OR STRING_FIELD NOT BETWEEN LOWER_BOUND_VALUE and UPPER_BOUND_VALUE)) ) END_IN_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
START_MAIN SELECT OUTER_BUCKET_NAME.* FROM BUCKET_NAME WHERE INNER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD EQUALS START_AGG_SUBQUERY ( SELECT RAW SUM(OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD) AS OUTER_SUBQUERY_AGG_FIELD FROM BUCKET_NAME USE KEYS META(OUTER_BUCKET_ALIAS).id WHERE (STRING_FIELD < STRING_VALUES) AND (((NUMERIC_FIELD IS NULL) AND (NUMERIC_FIELD >= NUMERIC_VALUE)) OR (NUMERIC_FIELD != NUMERIC_VALUE)) ) END_AGG_SUBQUERY END_MAIN;
